// ============non-terminal types=============
//  # => Integer
//  <assign> => Statement
//  <cast exp> => Exp
//  <class decl> => ClassDecl

//  <decl in class> => Decl

// ============productions (after empty-removal)=============
// 0: $$start ::= <start>
// 1: <start> ::= ws* <program>
// 2: <start> ::= <program>
// 3: <program> ::= <class decl>+
// 4: <class decl> ::= `class ID `{ <decl in class>* `}
// 5: <class decl> ::= `class ID `{ `}
// 6: <decl in class> ::= <method decl>
// 7: <method decl> ::= `public `void ID `( `) `{ <stmt>* `}
// 8: <method decl> ::= `public `void ID `( `) `{ `}
// 9: <type> ::= `int
// 10: <type> ::= `null
// 11: <type> ::= `void
// 12: <type> ::= `boolean
// 13: <type> ::= ID
// 14: <type> ::= <type> <empty bracket pair>
// 15: <empty bracket pair> ::= `[ `]
// 16: <stmt> ::= <assign> `;
// 17: <stmt> ::= `{ <stmt>* `}
// 18: <stmt> ::= `{ `}
// 19: <stmt> ::= <local var decl> `;
// 20: <stmt> ::= `break
// 21: <assign> ::= <exp> `= <exp>
// 22: <local var decl> ::= <type> ID `= <exp>
// 23: <exp> ::= <exp4>
// 24: <exp4> ::= `true
// 25: <exp4> ::= `false
// 26: <exp4> ::= <exp4> `+ <exp3>
// 27: <exp4> ::= <exp3>
// 28: <exp3> ::= <exp3> `* <exp2>
// 29: <exp3> ::= <exp3> `/ <exp2>
// 30: <exp3> ::= <exp3> `&& <exp2>
// 31: <exp3> ::= <exp2>
// 32: <exp2> ::= <cast exp>
// 33: <exp2> ::= <unary exp>
// 34: <cast exp> ::= `( <type> `) <cast exp>
// 35: <cast exp> ::= `( <type> `) <exp1>
// 36: <unary exp> ::= `- <unary exp>
// 37: <unary exp> ::= <exp1>
// 38: <exp1> ::= ID
// 39: <exp1> ::= <exp1> !<empty bracket pair> `[ <exp> `]
// 40: <exp1> ::= INTLIT
// 41: <exp1> ::= STRINGLIT
// 42: letter ::= {"A".."Z" "a".."z"}
// 43: letter128 ::= {193..218 225..250}
// 44: digit ::= {"0".."9"}
// 45: digit128 ::= {176..185}
// 46: any ::= {0..127}
// 47: any128 ::= {128..255}
// 48: ws ::= " "
// 49: ws ::= {10}
// 50: `boolean ::= "#" "b" "o" ws*
// 51: `boolean ::= "#" "b" "o"
// 52: `class ::= "#" "c" "l" ws*
// 53: `class ::= "#" "c" "l"
// 54: `void ::= "#" "v" "o" ws*
// 55: `void ::= "#" "v" "o"
// 56: `int ::= "#" "i" "t" ws*
// 57: `int ::= "#" "i" "t"
// 58: `break ::= "#" "b" "r" ws*
// 59: `break ::= "#" "b" "r"
// 60: `false ::= "#" "f" "a" ws*
// 61: `false ::= "#" "f" "a"
// 62: `true ::= "#" "t" "r" ws*
// 63: `true ::= "#" "t" "r"
// 64: `null ::= "#" "n" "u" ws*
// 65: `null ::= "#" "n" "u"
// 66: `public ::= "#" "p" "u" ws*
// 67: `public ::= "#" "p" "u"
// 68: `&& ::= "@" "&" ws*
// 69: `&& ::= "@" "&"
// 70: `* ::= "*" ws*
// 71: `* ::= "*"
// 72: `( ::= "(" ws*
// 73: `( ::= "("
// 74: `) ::= ")" ws*
// 75: `) ::= ")"
// 76: `{ ::= "{" ws*
// 77: `{ ::= "{"
// 78: `} ::= "}" ws*
// 79: `} ::= "}"
// 80: `- ::= "-" ws*
// 81: `- ::= "-"
// 82: `+ ::= "+" ws*
// 83: `+ ::= "+"
// 84: `= ::= "=" ws*
// 85: `= ::= "="
// 86: `[ ::= "[" ws*
// 87: `[ ::= "["
// 88: `] ::= "]" ws*
// 89: `] ::= "]"
// 90: `; ::= ";" ws*
// 91: `; ::= ";"
// 92: `/ ::= "/" ws*
// 93: `/ ::= "/"
// 94: ID ::= letter128 ws*
// 95: ID ::= letter128
// 96: ID ::= letter idChar* $$0
// 97: ID ::= letter $$0
// 98: INTLIT ::= {"1".."9"} digit* $$1
// 99: INTLIT ::= {"1".."9"} $$1
// 100: INTLIT ::= digit128 ws*
// 101: INTLIT ::= digit128
// 102: INTLIT ::= "0" hexDigit* $$2
// 103: INTLIT ::= "0" $$2
// 104: STRINGLIT ::= "@" '"' ws*
// 105: STRINGLIT ::= "@" '"'
// 106: STRINGLIT ::= '"' any* $$3
// 107: STRINGLIT ::= '"' $$3
// 108: idChar ::= letter
// 109: idChar ::= digit
// 110: idChar ::= "_"
// 111: idChar128 ::= letter128
// 112: idChar128 ::= digit128
// 113: idChar128 ::= {223}
// 114: hexDigit ::= {"0".."9" "A".."Z" "a".."z"}
// 115: hexDigit128 ::= {176..185 193..198 225..230}
// 116: digit* ::= digit* digit
// 117: digit* ::= digit
// 118: any* ::= any* any
// 119: any* ::= any
// 120: <decl in class>* ::= <decl in class>* <decl in class>
// 121: <decl in class>* ::= <decl in class>
// 122: hexDigit* ::= hexDigit* hexDigit
// 123: hexDigit* ::= hexDigit
// 124: <stmt>* ::= <stmt>* <stmt>
// 125: <stmt>* ::= <stmt>
// 126: idChar* ::= idChar* idChar
// 127: idChar* ::= idChar
// 128: <class decl>+ ::= <class decl>
// 129: <class decl>+ ::= <class decl>+ <class decl>
// 130: ws* ::= ws* ws
// 131: ws* ::= ws
// 132: $$0 ::= idChar128 ws*
// 133: $$0 ::= idChar128
// 134: $$1 ::= digit128 ws*
// 135: $$1 ::= digit128
// 136: $$2 ::= hexDigit128 ws*
// 137: $$2 ::= hexDigit128
// 138: $$3 ::= any128 ws*
// 139: $$3 ::= any128

**** STATE 0 ****
    $$start ::= <%> <start> // $
    -----------------------
    <class decl> ::= <%> `class [#] ID `{ <decl in class>* `} // $
    <class decl> ::= <%> `class [#] ID `{ <decl in class>* `} // <class decl>
    <class decl> ::= <%> `class [#] ID `{ [<decl in class>*] `} // $
    <class decl> ::= <%> `class [#] ID `{ [<decl in class>*] `} // <class decl>
    <class decl>+ ::= <%> <class decl> // $
    <class decl>+ ::= <%> <class decl> // <class decl>
    <class decl>+ ::= <%> <class decl>+ <class decl> // $
    <class decl>+ ::= <%> <class decl>+ <class decl> // <class decl>
    <program> ::= [#] <%> <class decl>+ // $
    <start> ::= <%> ws* <program> // $
    <start> ::= [ws*] <%> <program> // $
    `class ::= <%> "#" "c" "l" [ws*] // ID
    `class ::= <%> "#" "c" "l" ws* // ID
    ws ::= <%> " " // <program>
    ws ::= <%> " " // ws
    ws ::= <%> {10} [registerNewline] // <program>
    ws ::= <%> {10} [registerNewline] // ws
    ws* ::= <%> ws* ws // <program>
    ws* ::= <%> ws* ws // ws
    ws* ::= [ws*] <%> ws // <program>
    ws* ::= [ws*] <%> ws // ws
        <class decl>+ => shift: 55
        "#" => shift: 175
        ws => shift: 247
        <program> => shift: 137
        `class => shift: 83
        <start> => shift: 213
        ws* => shift: 278
        {10} => shift: 25
        " " => shift: 79
        <class decl> => shift: 199
